Important News

Incident of Japanese Navy Committing Murder in Hankou Escalates 61

Injured Ni Zhaomei Dies

Municipal Government Presents Three Conditions to Japanese Consulate

Hankou Correspondence: Regarding the case of Ni Zhaomei, a Chinese national, being shot by the Japanese Navy stationed in Hankou, the Hankou Municipal Government lodged a protest with the Japanese Consul on the 3rd, and conditions were being discussed. Unexpectedly, Ni died at 1:30 AM on the 4th at the Tongrenhui Hospital due to his severe injuries. The negotiations thus escalated. The Municipal Government has now presented three conditions, and the diplomatic inspector of the five provinces, Zhou Zechun, is personally negotiating with the Japanese Consul. Whether a smooth resolution can be achieved is still uncertain. The latest developments in the case are recorded separately below:

Ni Zhaomei Dies from Severe Injuries: Ni Zhaomei was injured on the morning of the 1st and was sent to the Japanese Concession Tongrenhui Hospital for treatment. At 4:00 PM, the hospital's doctor examined him in detail. The bullet entered from the left side of the waist and exited from the left side of the abdomen, with a small entry wound and a large exit wound. Although the injured person was unconscious, bleeding profusely, the doctor still believed he could be treated. He then used X-rays to examine the interior and stated that the abdominal bones were not severely damaged. He immediately issued a diagnosis certificate, which was signed and witnessed by a Japanese Navy translator. The thirteenth district director, Wan Dixiu, participated in the examination. He sent the hospital diagnosis certificate and the Japanese Navy translator's signature to the Public Security Bureau, which forwarded it to the Municipal Government for record. Unexpectedly, his condition worsened and worsened until 1:30 AM on the 4th, when he died from his injuries. Ni was 36 years old, extremely poor, and worked as a farmer.

Hankou Court Examines the Corpse: After Ni Zhaomei died, his younger brothers Ni Dongshan and Ni Zhenfang reported it to the thirteenth district. Director Wan immediately went to investigate and sent a letter to the Hankou District Court, requesting that it send someone to examine the body. At this time, Japanese Consul Tanaka also heard the news and rushed to the scene. Wan immediately made an informal statement to the Japanese Consul, stating that the Japanese side should bear full responsibility. He also stated to the deceased's relatives that he was willing to report to the authorities on their behalf and properly arrange for the funeral expenses and subsequent negotiations. The deceased's relatives agreed. After the prosecutor Liao Yuanxiang, dispatched by the court, conducted the examination, the body was temporarily taken away, awaiting government negotiations. Director Wan then went to the Municipal Government and reported the incident to Mayor Liu Wendao.

Japanese Consul Visits Mayor Liu: Japanese Consul-General Sakane Junzo (Tanaka), after receiving a report from the Tongrenhui Hospital, went to the Municipal Government with Vice-Consul Takai Suehiko at 10:00 AM to visit Mayor Liu Wendao. He personally described the incident and reported that Ni had died. He expressed great regret for this unfortunate incident, but said that the incident was not intentional by the Japanese Navy and asked for forgiveness. Mayor Liu immediately replied to the Consul that the Japanese Navy's armed crossing of the border, whether it was for target practice or hunting, whether intentional or unintentional, was a disregard for China's sovereignty and a contempt for Chinese lives. The Japanese side should be responsible. The Japanese Consul then left.

Presenting Conditions Such as Punishing the Culprit: After the Japanese Consul left, Mayor Liu immediately invited the five-province inspection commissioner Zhou Zechun to the government office and consulted with Secretary-General He Fuzhou, etc. In addition to immediately instructing the Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus to investigate the situation as soon as possible and submit a report, they decided to lodge a serious protest with the Japanese Consul. The conditions were: (1) Severely punish the murderer, (2) Provide generous compensation, and (3) Issue a formal apology. As for the issue of Japanese troops using live ammunition for target practice, because Japanese troops have done this in many parts of China in the past, they sent a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to inquire about how to negotiate and stop it. After the conditions were determined, it was 2:00 PM, and Commissioner Zhou Zechun went to visit the Japanese Consul for the first formal negotiation. It is reported that the Japanese Consul has given considerable answers to the requests made (April 4th).

Xu Yuanquan Arrives in Hankou 62

Hankou Correspondence: Xu Yuanquan, director of bandit suppression and rural pacification in the border area of Hunan, Hubei, and Sichuan, had to report to Director He of the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters on the situation of bandit suppression in western Hubei. On the 2nd of this month, he traveled down from the Shashi defense area on the Wuhu small steamer and arrived in Hankou on the morning of the 4th. The 10th Army's office in Hankou received Xu's departure telegram and sent a Feilong small steamship to meet him. Before reaching Jinkou, it encountered the Wuhu steamer, so they traveled east together downstream. At about 1:00 AM on the morning of the 4th, it arrived at Wharf No. 1 in Hankou. After Xu landed, he greeted the welcomers with a wave and took a car to the Third Army Group Headquarters to report to Director He on the bandit suppression situation in western Hubei and asked for instructions. Then, he visited Li Mingzhong, Liu Wendao, Wu Xingya, Xia Douyin, and former acquaintances in Hankou. In the afternoon, he returned to the 10th Army office in Hankou to rest. I then submitted my card and visited him at this time. I was received and had the following conversation: (Q) Western Hubei has been ravaged by the Red bandits for a long time. After your army's vigorous suppression, Jianli, Shishou, Tiaoxian, Hefeng, and Wufeng have been successively recovered. Has the remaining bandits been cleared? Xu (A) Since the various departments of our army have worked hard to suppress the Red bandits in western Hubei, both sides of the Yangtze River have been cleared. The scattered remnants of bandits lurking in various places have also been assigned teams to annihilate them. Now there is no problem with bandit suppression there. (Q) What is the situation of rural pacification in western Hubei now? (A) Since I took office as Director, I have ordered all counties in western Hubei and their subordinate troops to establish Rural Pacification Committees. Now the first step of rural pacification is underway, such as surveying the population and implementing Baojia, which are all being actively carried out. (Q) How was the inspection along the way on Director's trip to Hankou? (A) On this trip back to Hankou, I personally went ashore to inspect Tiaoguan, Chewan, and other places in Shishou to examine the discipline of our army and give instructions on methods to strictly protect the local area. Now Tiaoguan has built extremely solid fortifications to prevent bandits from returning from the border of Hunan. (Q) What is the situation in Jingzhou and Shashi? (A) Jingzhou and Shashi are very peaceful, and business is also quite prosperous, which is very different from when I first arrived. (Q) After Director visits Director He in Hankou, will you need to go to Beijing? (A) I will not stay elsewhere for the time being. I will stay in Hankou for a while and then return to my defense area. At this point, I excused myself and left (April 4th).

Mutiny in Luchuan Resolved 63

Taiyuan Correspondence: The remnants of the mutineers in Changzhi fled east and disturbed the vicinity of Lingchuan. According to telegram reports from division commanders Yang Xiaou and Yan Shi, the Lingchuan mutiny was suppressed after troops were sent to pursue and suppress them. Lingchuan was recovered on March 29, and the remaining bandits fled to the towns near the city. Troops are still being sent to pursue and suppress them, and it is expected that it will be cleared soon. The original telegrams are as follows: (1) "It is reported by Lv Chaoran, battalion commander of the Wang Sitian regiment under my command, that after I was ordered to vigorously suppress the remnants of the bandits in Lingchuan and arrived at Pingcheng Town, north of Lingchuan, I led my troops to Lingchuan at 10:00 PM on the afternoon of the reconnaissance. We reached the destination at 1:30 AM and carried out a vigorous suppression. At 2:00 AM, we captured Butterfly Mountain. The bandits were unable to resist and fled to the towns near the city. Dozens of bandits were killed. Lingchuan has now been recovered. In addition to tracking and pursuing them to the towns near the city, I am sending a telegram to report. I have ordered the battalion commander to quickly pursue and suppress them so that they can be cleared as soon as possible to secure the countryside and report their merits. I respectfully report." (2) "The situation of Lv Chaoran's battalion of the Wang Sitian regiment of my command, defeating the remnants of bandits in the city of Lingchuan and tracking them to the towns near the city, has been reported in the telegrams. In addition to ordering Lv battalion commander to supervise the troops and Jiang's regiment and Hao's battalion to quickly annihilate them and prevent them from spreading, I respectfully report first."

According to other news, the mutineers in Changzhi and Jiangxian are still being dealt with. According to a person from Pianguan County, a company of the security team stationed in the county also mutinied a few days ago and fled to the border with weapons. The Yang Yaofang army stationed in Qixian has not been very bad since it arrived, and the local people are living in peace as always. Unexpectedly, a small part (about dozens of people) of the county town garrison suddenly fled to Wenshui County with weapons. The army division headquarters received the news and immediately sent a large battalion to pursue them. The fleeing soldiers looted every village in Wenshui County. Because they had not gone far, they were caught up by the troops sent to pursue them. The mutineers were surrounded, and both sides exchanged fire for several hours. As a result, except for a few soldiers who escaped, they have all been dealt with. The ringleader was captured and, after interrogation, was shot outside the south gate of the county. (March 31)

Liaoning Provincial Government Makes Great Efforts to Maintain Banknotes 64

Recalling Provincial Banknotes and Reorganizing the Provincial Bank

Urging the Central Government to Approve Financial Public Bonds

Taiyuan Correspondence: Since the provincial banknotes plummeted repeatedly a few days ago, society has been quite uneasy. Each silver dollar once exchanged for more than three yuan and three jiao in banknotes. Subsequently, the provincial government made great efforts to maintain the value, on the one hand, implementing crackdowns on small money stalls along the streets, and on the other hand, ordering banks and various silver firms and money shops to cooperate. Only in the past two days has the market gradually recovered, with each yuan rising from over three yuan back to two yuan eight or nine jiao. Officials have been negotiating for days and decided on several methods of raising funds, and the funds raised in the future will be used exclusively for recalling provincial banknotes. As for the method of recalling, it will be done through secretly buying at market prices. At the same time, the official fixed minimum price is expected to be no less than 40% of the face value. Together with the provincial banknotes withdrawn for monthly cash redemption, they will be burned and destroyed. In the future, the required military expenses, in addition to requesting assistance from Deputy Commander Zhang, will have to be obtained through other means and will no longer be borrowed from the provincial bank.

As for the provincial bank, officials recently plan to attract commercial shares for reorganization due to its excessive debts, and it will still be jointly operated by officials and merchants. Branch offices will be established in each county, guaranteed by the chamber of commerce. First-class counties will issue 500,000 yuan of banknotes, second-class counties will issue 400,000 yuan of banknotes, and third-class counties will issue 300,000 yuan of banknotes, using the newly issued banknotes to absorb the old provincial banknotes. Some people also advocate using foreign capital to exploit mineral resources, borrowing some foreign capital first for the purpose of reorganizing the provincial banknotes. However, this plan is still under close discussion.

Recently, Shang Zhen, in order to earnestly request the central government to approve the issuance of Shanxi Financial Public Bonds, telegraphed the central government and Deputy Commander Zhang. The original text is recorded as follows: (1) "Urgent, Nanjing Executive Yuan, I respectfully request that the case of reorganizing Shanxi Financial Public Bonds, which I requested to be restored, was previously opened by the Office of Civil Servants and sent to your court for handling, etc. I am extremely grateful for the central government's deep concern for Shanxi Province. Recently, businessmen and people in Shanxi Province, because this public bond has not yet been clearly restored by decree, rumors have arisen, and the price of provincial banknotes has plummeted. Upon investigation, Shanxi Province's currency is unified, and there is nothing else that can replace provincial banknotes. With the price of banknotes being low and the price of goods rising, the daily life of the people has been affected. Moreover, after the reorganization of the army, there is still no source of income for the salaries. Although the province is勉struggling to raise rations, the amount is small and the value is low, insufficient to provide a full meal. The military and civilians are in a state of panic, with a sense of impending doom. I earnestly implore your court to consider the critical situation in Shanxi Province and approve the issuance of the aforementioned financial public bonds as soon as possible to stabilize the people's hearts. I am overwhelmed with anticipation. Shang Zhen, Chairman of the Shanxi Provincial Government, respectfully kowtows." (2) "Urgent, Shenyang Deputy Commander Zhang, I have received your confidential telegram. The price of provincial banknotes in Shanxi Province has plummeted in recent days, and the value is already below 30% of face value. The military and civilians are in a state of panic, with a sense of impending doom. Although the reasons for this are complex, the main reason is that the method of military pay has not been determined, and the provincial banknotes have no guarantee. Now that the reorganization loan has been compromised, I earnestly request that you immediately order the remittance of funds. With these funds to regulate the market in Taiyuan, the price of banknotes may be stabilized. Furthermore, in order to maintain the provincial banknotes, I telegraphed the central government on the Qing Day of last month, requesting that the reorganization of Shanxi Financial Public Bonds of 24 million yuan be approved for restoration. This case has been submitted to the President of the Executive Yuan for handling. I earnestly implore Your Excellency to urge the Executive Yuan to approve the issuance as soon as possible to stabilize the people's hearts. I am overwhelmed with anticipation. Shang Zhen respectfully kowtows." (March 31st)

The Question of the Jiaoji Railway Building the Daoji Branch Line 65

The Jiaoji Railway Plans to Build to Linqing First

The Shandong Provincial Government Will Also Make Suggestions to the Central Government

Jinan Correspondence: Regarding the extension of the Jiaoji Railway to Daokou, Ge Guangting, Chairman of the Jiaoji Railway Committee, is currently in Beijing for negotiations and has already obtained the consent of the Ministry of Railways. According to Mr. Ge, the Jiaoji Railway currently has only more than 400 kilometers, but it has a huge debt of 40 million Japanese yen. If revenue is not increased, I am afraid that it will still not be redeemed when the deadline expires. This will not only result in the loss of rights and interests but also be looked down upon internationally. Therefore, extending to the most suitable Daokou is indeed necessary. However, extending from Jinan to Daokou is a total of 300 kilometers, and there is no such huge amount of money available for the time being. It is now planned to be divided into three phases. The first phase is to build to Linqing first, which is about 100 kilometers long, and is estimated to require 7 million yuan. According to the planned plan, the steel rails freed up by this road can be laid, which can save half of the cost, and only 3.5 million yuan needs to be raised through bonds to be sufficient for use. After the first phase of the extension line is completed, business will commence, and the income from the business will be used to continue to build the second and third phases. If the entire Daoji line is completed, then this road will be more than 700 kilometers long, and it will be able to issue 40 million in public bonds to redeem this road at once. However, this matter is of great importance and depends entirely on the efforts of the people, etc. Furthermore, today (the 3rd) at the Shandong Provincial Government's regular meeting, Wang Fangting, Director of the Department of Agriculture and Mines, also proposed the construction of the Daoji Railway. It has been resolved to submit it to the central government for approval. The proposal is recorded as follows: "For the proposal, revitalizing local industries and promoting social prosperity are not limited to one end. The development of transportation agencies is the most urgent task. Based on my limited understanding, the construction of the Daoji Railway is a crucial plan for this province. Upon investigation, Daokou Town in Weihui, Henan, is located on the south bank of the Wei River, connecting Jixian to the west, Tianjin to the north, and more than 400 miles east of Jinan. In the past, it was an important route for transporting grains from Yan, Lu, and Yu. The people of Shandong benefited greatly from the goods transported from Daokou to Shandong. Since the Pinghan and Jinpu Railways were successively created, the commercial transport between Lu and Yu has taken a roundabout turn, and the prosperity between Daokou and Jinan is no longer what it used to be. Now, if a railway is built from Daokou to Jinan, it will connect a horizontal line in the middle of the two vertical lines of the Pinghan and Jinpu Railways, making transportation between Lu and Yu direct. Moreover, it will connect the Daoji Railway with the Daoqing Railway. The convenience of this is self-evident. Furthermore, Daokou is adjacent to Zhangde and Xinxiang, which are also strategically important places. Once this road is opened, its impact will not only be related to the industrial prosperity of Shandong. It is proposed that the provincial government submit a request to the central government, ordering the Ministry of Railways and the Construction Committee to send personnel to survey, establish a plan, and implement it quickly. The local area will be very fortunate." (April 3rd)

Newly Established Seven Counties in Qinghai 67

Qinghai is located in the upper reaches of the Yellow River, bordering Gansu to the northeast, Sichuan, Xikang, and Tibet to the south, and Xinjiang to the west. It covers a vast area of approximately 2.49 million square miles, with a population of approximately one million. The mountains and rivers are closely connected, and the terrain is completely secure. The climate is extremely cold and hot, and the products are abundant, and breeding is quite rapid. Last month, Wang Yutang, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs of the province, submitted a request to the Ministry of Interior to add seven counties, namely, Gonghe, Manyuan, Tongren, Huzhu, Minhe, Yushu, and Dulan, due to the vast territory of Qinghai, the gradual increase in population, the excessively large jurisdiction of the old counties, and the inconvenience of administration. The Ministry of Interior has submitted the request to the Executive Yuan, which was approved at the 17th State Council meeting on the 24th of last month, allowing the establishment. The boundaries of the newly established counties are investigated as follows: Gonghe County, east to Jiangla·Luoyi Village, connecting Xining·Bayen, west to Qieji·Duoerma Sheep Bend, connecting Dahe Dam, south to the Yellow River, connecting Guide, northeast to Riyue Mountain·Laji Mountain, connecting Xining, northwest to Wenbozhai·Shijia Mountain, bordering Qinghai. The north-south distance is more than 120 li, and the east-west distance is more than 310 li.

Manyuan County, the east is bounded by the Laerjia Mountain Ridge and Yongdeng County, Gansu, the west is bounded by Babao Mountain, the south is bounded by Dasaka Mountain and Datong, the north is bounded by Daxue Mountain and Shiliangzhou, Gansu, and the southeast is bounded by Tangritou Mountain and the Ganchen Temple in Huzhu County. The north-south distance is more than 130 li, and the east-west distance is more than 380 li.

Tongren County, the Baoan Fort area under the jurisdiction of Xunhua County is vast and has a complex population. It is 140 li away from the seat of Xunhua County, and the rule is extremely inconvenient. Therefore, Tongren County was added.

Minhe County, the west side, (1) the dividing point of Laoya is set at the mouth of Lucao Gully. Hula Lotus Terrace east of the mouth is under the jurisdiction of Minhe, and the land west of the mouth is under the jurisdiction of Ledu. (2) The dividing point south of the Huangshui River starts from the mouth of Lucao Gully and extends to Daxue Mountain, with villages as the boundary. Villages such as Xiaquan, Guojiazhuang, Xujiashan, Shuangkulongshan, Qinjiazhuang, Daxingziwan, Xiawomuchi, Shirenzhuang, Benkengwan, Tiejiazhuang, Zhuazha, and Ganchi have their original boundaries under the jurisdiction of Minhe. Shangmachang, Hanjiaquan, Yuanjiaquan, Jinjiadapo, Shangwomuchi, Hongzhuanggou and other villages have their original boundaries under the jurisdiction of Ledu. (3) The dividing point north of the Huangshui River starts from the north side of the Lotus Terrace Temple and extends eastward to the mouth of Qiaogou Gully, then follows the gully northward to the Gou'nao·Ganwangjiamiao Ridge. Villages such as Ganwangjia, Luojiawan, Xilakutu, Guoguo, Xinzhuangzi, Kuandulan, Zhuangzigou, and Nalonggou are under the jurisdiction of Minhe. Villages such as Bagongwan, Shashitai, Quanerwan, Mao Yan etc. are under the jurisdiction of Ledu. The northeast borders Yongdeng County in Gansu, the east borders Yongjing County, the south borders Linxia County, and the southwest borders Bayen County in this province. The north-south distance varies from 150 li to 100 li, and the east-west distance varies from 100 li to 60 li.

Huzhu County, the boundary on the west side of Juyun Guchuan·Dongshanding extends southeast to Houzi River. Villages such as Xinzhuang, Nanse, Chenjia, and Daijia to the north are under the jurisdiction of Huzhu, and Houzi River is under the jurisdiction of Xining. Tianjiazhuang east of the Beichuan River and Kuozebu to the north (the fort has four villages, namely, Hongya Zhuang, Kangjia Zhuang, Hetan Zhuang, and Wangjia Zhuang) are under the jurisdiction of Xining. Sunhan Fort to the north (the fort has two villages, namely, Sunjia Zhuang and Hanjia Mountain) is under the jurisdiction of Huzhu. Starting from the mouth of Houzi River, the southeast extends to Hetangchuan Estuary north of the Huangshui River. Xiaosai is under the jurisdiction of Xining, and Yunjia Kou and Fujia Sai are under the jurisdiction of Huzhu. The southern part starts from the Hetangchuan Estuary, and all the land north of the Huangshui River (such as Gaosai, Baimasi, and Zhangqisai) extends to Ledu, which is the boundary and under the jurisdiction of Huzhu. The east borders Ledu and Yongdeng County in Gansu, the north connects Manyuan County, the northwest connects Datong, and the south crosses the Huangshui River and connects Xining. The distance from south to north is more than 70 li, and the distance from east to west is 86 li.

In addition, the administrative areas of Yushu and Dulan counties have not yet been ascertained.

Legislative Yuan Revises the Articles of the County Self-Defense Corps Law 68

At its 138th meeting yesterday (the 4th), the Legislative Yuan passed the revised articles 4, 6, 9 and 10 of the County Self-Defense Corps Law, as follows: (Article 4) The organization of the self-defense corps in each county shall be one pai per neighborhood, with the neighborhood chief as the pai chief, one jia per township or town, with the township chief or town chief as the jia chief, one district group per district, with the district chief as the district group leader, and the county as the general group, with the county magistrate as the general group leader. The general group, district group, and jia pai may all establish deputy chiefs when necessary to handle affairs. (Article 6) The deputy chief of the general group shall be appointed by the general group leader and reported to the provincial government for record. (Article 9) The seal of the general group of the self-defense corps shall be issued by the provincial government, and the seals of the district groups and jia pai shall be issued by the general group leader, but they shall not be affixed for matters unrelated to self-defense. (Article 10) The seals of the self-defense corps shall all be made of wood, and their style shall be determined by the Ministry of Interior.

First General Assembly of the Asian Cultural Association 69

Based on the Spirit of the Three Principles of the People

Seeking the Asian Cultural Revival Movement

Aims to Gather People from All Over the World

Organize the International of the Three Principles of the People

Nanjing Express News: At 9:00 a.m. on the 5th, the Asian Cultural Association held its first general assembly at the Zhizhi Hall of the National Central University. The representatives attending the meeting included representatives from Goryeo, Taiwan, India, Siam, Annam, Burma, and Nanjing, Shanghai, Peiping, Guangzhou, Hankou, and other places in China, as well as representatives from various organizations and guests, totaling more than 400 people. The presidium consisted of five people: Huang Shaomei, Tao Linying (China), Mingsheng (India), Li Shizhong (Goryeo), and Peng Ziming (Taiwan). Huang Shaomei, the chairman, gave an opening speech after the ceremony, followed by Tao Linying's report on the preparations, followed by reports from the representatives. Finally, the guests gave speeches, and then the election of the executive and supervisory committee members of the association began. A declaration, general regulations, and many important cases were passed on the spot. Finally, the meeting ended with slogans and photography. After the meeting, the representatives went to Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum to lay flowers and pay their respects. The chairman's opening speech and report are recorded on the left.

Chairman's Opening Speech: Distinguished representatives, distinguished guests, fellow comrades, in the "vast and boundless" and "all-encompassing" universe, many star systems are brilliantly displayed. Among the many star systems, there is a solar system with the sun as its main body. Among the planets that revolve around the sun, there is the earth on which we humans live. On the earth, in the five continents, there is Asia. In the Zhizhi Hall of the National Central University in Nanjing, Republic of China, on April 5, 1931, the first general assembly of the Asian Cultural Association is being held. At this assembly, there are representatives of the Chinese people, representatives of the Indian people, representatives of the Korean people, representatives of the Taiwanese people, representatives of the Annamese people, and representatives of other oppressed peoples of Asia. Everyone is determined to promote Asian culture and develop Asian culture. Everyone is determined to seek independence and freedom for all peoples. Everyone is prepared to participate in and promote this great and arduous task with the full strength of each nation. In such an enthusiastic revolutionary atmosphere, we have infinite joy and infinite hope.

Distinguished representatives of the oppressed peoples, since the European Industrial Revolution, capitalists in Europe and the United States, possessing huge capital, applying scientific methods, and using new-style production mechanisms to exploit the wages earned by the majority of toiling masses in society through blood and sweat, have formed a situation in which a small number of capitalists monopolize all economic privileges and control all political power, thus becoming international capitalist imperialists. They control the tragic fate of the vast majority of human beings. They directly and indirectly carry out political, economic, and even cultural aggression against all small and weak nations. They boast of their own culture, but in reality, the essence of their culture is only material aggression. Their culture is simply a culture of "things" rather than a culture of "people." In the modern world, the culture of "things" has replaced the culture of "people." How painful and terrible this is!

Distinguished representatives, we have all been invaded by world capitalist imperialists. We are naturally very clear about the above facts, and the impression in our minds is naturally particularly profound. Let us take a look at what our Asian culture was like in the past. When Premier Sun Yat-sen traveled north alone, he detoured to Kobe, Japan, and gave a speech entitled Greater Asianism, in which he said, "Our Asia is the birthplace of the most ancient culture. Thousands of years ago, the people of Asia had already attained a very high level of culture." He also said, "Fundamentally speaking, European culture in the last hundred years is a scientific culture that emphasizes utilitarianism. When this culture is applied to human society, there is only material civilization, only airplanes and bombs, only foreign guns and cannons. It is simply a culture of force. Europeans have recently used this culture of force to oppress our Asia, so our Asia cannot progress. This culture that specializes in using force to oppress people is acting tyrannically. Therefore, European culture is a culture of tyranny. But we in the East have always looked down on the culture of tyranny. There is another culture that is better than the culture of tyranny. The essence of this culture is benevolence, righteousness, morality, and the way of the king. Therefore, Asian culture is a culture of the way of the king." Premier Sun's precise and thorough remarks, in dissecting European and Asian cultures, not only clearly exposed the weaknesses of European culture but also revealed the advantages and characteristics of Asian culture.

In Asia, not only the Chinese nation, which values loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace, can represent Asian culture, but also the Indian nation's gentleness and intelligence, as well as the magnanimity and peace of other nations, everywhere express the characteristics of Asian culture. If we look through history, whether it is Chinese culture, Indian culture, Turkestan culture, or the entire Asian culture, all have supreme value and glory. These historical records give us ironclad examples.

Looking at it comparatively, European culture is a culture that makes the majority of people in the world groan in pain, a culture that has emerged in the last hundred years or so, a culture of "things," a culture of tyranny. Asian culture is a culture with the characteristics of liberating all oppressed nations, a culture with a long history and past glory, a culture of "people," a culture of the way of the king. Therefore, when we look at the people in the world who are suffering, when we look at the oppressed nations of Asia, we should use Asian culture to relieve the poverty of European culture. We should use Asian culture to resist European culture. The first step we should take is to promote Asian culture and develop Asian culture under this international organization of the Asian Cultural Association. We should further understand the Three Principles of the People established by Premier Sun, and everywhere make the happiness and equality of mankind the basis for cultural construction. This is precisely the synthesis of the great achievements of Asian culture to meet the modern environment. We should unanimously base ourselves on the principles of the Three Principles of the People, unite the nations of the world that treat each other equally, organize the international of the Three Principles of the People, revive Asian culture, and complete the great unity of the world.

Distinguished representatives, fellow comrades, I have spoken at length. Now, let me summarize a few important points below: (1) We should recognize that what conquers small and weak nations by force and inflicts cruelty on the entire human race is European culture, the savage and tyrannical culture of "things." (2) We should further recognize that what has the spirit of liberating oppressed nations and saving mankind from danger is Asian culture, the peaceful and royal culture of "people." (3) Our most recent efforts should be to promote Asian culture and develop Asian culture in order to resist the European savage and tyrannical culture of "things." (4) To revive Asian culture, to save oppressed nations, to liberate oppressed nations, and to relieve the suffering of all mankind, we can only do so by basing ourselves on the principles of the Three Principles of the People, uniting the nations of Asia and the world, organizing the national international of the Three Principles of the People, and taking on the responsibility of realizing the great unity of the world. Distinguished representatives, fellow comrades, our responsibilities are extremely heavy, our work is extremely arduous, and we should advance vigorously step by step with a spirit of sacrifice and a determination to fight. We believe that our final efforts will surely lead to final success. Let us work hard from now on and continue to work hard.

Report to all representatives and comrades, after a long period of hard work, the Asian Cultural Association has come to an end and is holding its inaugural meeting today. This is a very worthy celebration. It is a rare opportunity for representatives from all over the world to come here to attend the meeting and gather together. Now, I would like to take this opportunity to briefly report to you on the preparations for this association. The culture of the world today can be clearly seen as one that is a culture of "people," namely Asian culture, which speaks of the way of the king, and one that is a culture of "things," namely European culture, which speaks of the way of the hegemon. These two fundamentally conflicting and incompatible cultures have formed two different stages in the world. According to the current situation, it is said that the culture of people has been suppressed by the culture of things, that is, European culture suppresses Asian culture. However, from a theoretical point of view, Asian culture is the oldest and most beautiful culture in the world. It is not that we ourselves are exaggerating, but that no one with a little knowledge in European countries dares to deny it. However, we Asians have neglected it too much. We have not continued to carry forward the position and value of Asian culture in the world. We have only held onto the concept of conservatism, and as a result, it has become increasingly depressed. We feel that this danger is a major obstacle to the problem of Asian cultural revival. Therefore, there is a motivation to unite comrades from Asian countries to organize this association. Comrades from Asian countries can understand this principle as a matter of great pain, and they all have the same feeling. Therefore, they have risen up in response and organized branch offices and liaison offices everywhere. It is estimated that branch offices and liaison offices have been established in the South Seas Islands, Europe, America, Canada, Japan, Korea, Taiwan, India, Siam, Annam, Burma, etc. In China, there are Guangdong, Hankou, Shanghai, Peiping, etc. The total number of members is about 50,000. Recently, those who are enthusiastically joining have been coming one after another. This grand occasion has opened a new era of Asian national unity. This is something that can be reported to all representatives. I think all the representatives present today must be very happy. The purpose of today's first general assembly is, on the one hand, to take this opportunity to elect formal executive and supervisory committee members, so that they can truly shoulder the mission of this association and seek the development of its affairs. On the other hand, it is to understand the situation of branch offices in various places, to check the work of the past, to exchange opinions with each other, and to jointly seek the development of its affairs. At the same time, it is also to unite the strength of our Asian nations and to complete the world cultural revolution as the goal. It is hoped that all the representatives attending the meeting will contribute their opinions as much as possible to achieve perfection. However, the time for this preparation was very short, and the abilities of the comrades were limited. Perhaps there are some shortcomings in all the procedures. There may also be some shortcomings in the hospitality for the representatives. It is hoped that all the representatives will forgive and forgive.

Liaoning Construction Department Merged into the Department of Agriculture 70

Peng Jiqun Resigns as Director of the Construction Department to Focus on Party Affairs

The Duties of the Construction Department Are Concurrently Handled by Liu Heling, Director of the Department of Agriculture

Shenyang Correspondence: Peng Jiqun, Director of the Liaoning Construction Department, is skilled in engineering knowledge. Last year, when the Northeast opened Huludao Port, Zhang Xueliang knew of Peng's ability and ordered him to concurrently serve as Director of the Port Affairs Office, supervising the entire port project. Peng rushed between Shenyang and Huludao, taking care of both and making many plans. This time, the central government ordered Peng to be the Party Affairs Guidance Committee Member of Liaoning Province. Peng believed that the work of party affairs was important, and in order to focus on party affairs, he submitted a request to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee to resign from his position as Director of the Construction Department. The request was approved by the Party Affairs Committee. The vacant position of Director of the Construction Department was ordered to be concurrently held by Liu Heling, Director of the Department of Agriculture and Mines. In order to facilitate command, the Construction Department was moved into the Department of Agriculture in Yijing Road to work. Preparations have been underway for several days and have already made some progress. The handover has also been completed. The Construction Department officially merged into the Department of Agriculture to work from April 1st. (April 1st)

Change of Head of the Special Police Department of Harbin 71

Bowen Yue promoted to Deputy Chief of Staff

Wang Ruihua Appointed as Successor

Harbin Correspondence: Following the promotion of Bowen Yue, the head of the Special Police Department, to Deputy Chief of Staff, the vacant position has been filled by Wang Ruihua, recommended by the Northeast Political Committee and formerly the Director of Education at the Liaoning Main Campus of the Northeast Military Academy. The appointment was made by the Special District Executive Officer's Office. On the 31st, Wang arrived in Harbin from Shenyang with six staff members, and officially took office on April 1st. Many of the previous personnel have been replaced, except for those who are senior and experienced in police administration. New appointments include Hou Zhizhong as Secretary-General, Sun Puwen as Head of the Fourth Section, Yin Dongjiao as Head of the Fifth Section, Wang Ziqi as Director of the License Division, and Xu Rongjiu as Assistant Inspector-General. It is said that the heads of various bureaus and teams will also be replaced. Wang is currently 40 years old, a native of Guixi, Liaoning, now residing in Xingcheng. He graduated from the Wu Peifu Military Academy and served as a platoon and company commander in Xu Shuzheng's Border Defense Army. After the Zhili-Anhui War, he served as a deputy battalion commander in Wang Chengbin's 23rd Division. In the eleventh year, he returned to Fengtian, serving as an instructor in the Training Corps, a brigade commander of the Fourth Supplementary Brigade, a brigade commander of the 27th Brigade, a deputy army commander of the Ninth Army, a garrison commander of Koubei, and a deputy army commander of the Eighth Army. He was recently transferred from Director of Education at the Liaoning Main Campus of the Northeast Military Academy to Head of the Special Police Department. Before Wang was appointed as the head of the Special Police Department, Jia Wenqi, the former deputy head of the department, and Yu Jingtao, the deputy head of the Road Police Department, were the most active contenders. Their strengths were evenly matched, and neither was willing to give way. Unexpectedly, the result was that Wang got the position. In Harbin, there is a saying, "Director Jia was originally not fake (賈處長原來不假), and Yu was ambitious but lacked the strength (于有心而力未餘)," which is an interesting anecdote about the appointment of the head of the Special Police Department. (April 1st)

Investigation into the Reduction of Freight Rates by the South Manchuria Railway 72

Rates Still Higher Than Chinese Railways

No Impact on Chinese Railways

Shenyang Correspondence: The South Manchuria Railway, operated by the Japanese in the Northeast, has generated astonishing profits over the years. Even with the high gold prices and reduced transportation last year, the railway's income was still considerable. However, because the profits were not as high as in previous years, the Japanese claimed that the impact was due to the efforts of the Northeast authorities in railway construction and the price reduction of joint transportation on the Northeast railways. Recently, they have harbored the intention of undermining this and, as a result of discussions by the South Manchuria Railway Company authorities, have implemented a reduction in the freight rates for special products between Shenyang and Yingkou, changing to a silver standard, and extending this to Andong and Dalian. From mid-March to the end of September, the freight rates for special products shipped from Shenyang and various stations to Andong and Dalian will be temporarily reduced. A comparison of the new and old freight rates for the major stations along the South Manchuria Railway is as follows: (1) Shenyang: The current freight rate is 7.76 yuan per ton, and the newly revised rate is 5.76 yuan. (2) Kaiyuan: The current freight rate is 9.94 yuan per ton, and the newly revised rate is 7.94 yuan. (3) Sipingjie: The current freight rate is 11.99 yuan per ton, and the newly revised rate is 9.99 yuan. However, it remains doubtful whether the implementation of these specific price reductions will have a real effect. Even with Changchun as the starting point for goods exported to Dalian, Kobe, and Shanghai, the freight rates are still higher than those of the Chinese railways. Therefore, although the Japanese are trying to counter Chinese railways, the Chinese railways may not be significantly affected. The differences between Chinese and Japanese freight rates are as follows: (1) South Manchuria Railway: From Changchun to Dalian, the rate is 375.9 yuan (Japanese currency) per ton. Chinese Railway: From Changchun via Siping, Taonan, Yingkou to Dalian, the rate is 362.9 yuan (Japanese currency) per ton. Thus, the Chinese route from Changchun to Dalian is about 13 yuan cheaper (in Japanese currency) than the South Manchuria Railway route. (2) South Manchuria Railway: From Changchun via Dalian to Kobe, the rate is 451.4 yuan (Japanese currency) per ton. Chinese Railway: From Changchun via Yingkou to Kobe, the rate is 441.39 yuan (Japanese currency) per ton. Thus, the Chinese route from Changchun to Kobe is about 10.01 yuan cheaper (in Japanese currency) than the South Manchuria Railway route. (3) South Manchuria Railway: From Changchun via Dalian to Shanghai, the rate is 451.4 yuan (Japanese currency) per ton. Chinese Railway: From Changchun via Yingkou to Shanghai, the rate is 440.8 yuan (Japanese currency) per ton. Thus, the Chinese route from Changchun to Shanghai is about 10.6 yuan cheaper (in Japanese currency) than the South Manchuria Railway route. (29th)

Wu Tiecheng's Speech on the Northeast under Japanese and Russian Aggression (Continued) 73

As for Japan's aggression against our Northeast, it has become an undeniable fact. They have historical, diplomatic, and factual bases. They take all the so-called rights of succession, unequal treaties, financial institutions, etc., with the South Manchuria Railway as the center, and steadily advance their policy of aggression. They even completely changed the local names and regarded the Northeast as the Japanese's Manchuria and Mongolia. Not only that, in addition to the special establishment of various political and cultural invasion agencies along the South Manchuria Railway, they even set up fortresses across borders in military terms, and even carried out cross-border activities in police terms. They also declared themselves to be maintaining law and order for China and exposing reactionary elements for China. Isn't this turning the guest into the host and despising China's sovereignty? Speaking of the economic aggression of the Japanese, it goes without saying. Most of everything we need in our daily lives in the Northeast is Japanese. Although China also has several banks in terms of financial institutions, the driving force that dominates finance is entirely in the hands of Japanese banks. The same is true for industry, commerce, export, and import, all of which are controlled by the Japanese. Even our lives are almost in the hands of the Japanese. This is a very dangerous thing. It seems that the prices in the Northeast are several times more expensive than those inside the customs, because the economic organization, such as industry and commerce, uses the Japanese gold standard. The Northeast, which is vast and rich in resources, has now been reduced to gold price confusion and food shortages, which can be said to be completely dominated by Japanese imperialism. Since the Japanese have this status in the Northeast, their so-called special interests naturally go beyond the scope of the private transactions between Japan and Russia at that time. Originally, the Japanese's so-called special interests were the inheritance of the so-called vested interests of Imperial Russia when Japan defeated Imperial Russia. But what is it now? Isn't it already more than ten thousand times the vested interests of Imperial Russia at that time? Looking at the above situation as a whole, since the Northeast is in such a siege of imperialist encirclement on all sides, in order to save China, we must first rescue the Northeast from the joint attack of Japan and Russia. In order to achieve freedom and equality, we must first enrich the Northeast, the gateway of China, and make it complete. Now, according to my humble opinion, we should have the following determination and attention:

Regarding the negative aspects: (1) Japan must abandon its so-called special interests in Manchuria and Mongolia. Before it has actually abandoned them, it must be prevented from developing and expanding the scope of its interests in Manchuria and Mongolia. (2) After the abolition, all agreements between Japan and any third country regarding Japan's position in Manchuria and Mongolia must be terminated at the same time, and Japan must be prevented from having any agreements of the same nature with third countries. (3) We must strengthen our defenses and prevent the Han Chinese traitors from privately granting the rights to all forests, mines, and land to the Japanese. (4) Before the recovery of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Soviet Russia must sincerely fulfill the Sino-Russian-Fengtian Agreement, and the principle of equality must be followed in the employment and administration of the Chinese Eastern Railway. (5) Before the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, Soviet Russia must guarantee that it will not promote communism in China, endanger China's national system, and use money to buy Chinese bandits to transform into communists to disrupt China's security. Even after the resumption of diplomatic relations, if there are still communist bandits found to be rioting in China, Soviet Russia cannot shirk its responsibility to the Third International. (6) A thorough study should be conducted on the issue of trade, because Russian commerce is state-operated, while Chinese commerce is privately operated. The two sides should discuss the fairest and most appropriate method to ensure that Chinese private commerce in Russia is not destroyed by Soviet Russian state-operated commerce. (7) Soviet Russia should immediately cease all actions to incite and control Outer Mongolia and withdraw the Soviet Russian troops stationed in Outer Mongolia.

The above are the negative measures, which are also the measures that should be taken to deal with imperialism. As for the positive measures, they are designed to build China, especially the Northeast, that is, to concentrate all our strength to develop the resources of the Northeast, that is, forests, minerals, and immigration to reclaim wasteland, to enrich the Northeast, and to ensure that there is not an inch of space and leakage on the ground in the Northeast, so that imperialists have no opportunity to invade. However, whether it is negatively dealing with imperialists or actively planning the construction of China, especially the Northeast, we must stand on the basis of unity, peace, stability, and national unity, and then the abolition of unequal treaties and the construction of China will have the hope and grasp of success. In other words, China is not unified, not peaceful, or falsely unified and falsely peaceful, and it is impossible to abolish unequal treaties and plan the construction of China. Since the National Diplomacy Association was established to save China, especially to save the Northeast, it should, in accordance with the Prime Minister's will, first awaken all the people of the Northeast to seek the most violent and dangerous Japanese and Russian invasion, which is the most powerful way to resist imperialism, because even if countries such as Britain, France, Italy, and the United States are willing to abandon unequal treaties, Japan still wants to maintain its special interests, and Soviet Russia still cannot stop its conspiracy against the Northeast, then the Northeast will not be free for a day, and China will not be independent for a day. Today's Northeast is like the throat of a person in China, and has a relationship of life and death. The future prosperity and decline of China's national fortune and the growth and decline of national power are directly affected by the solution of the Northeast issue. Today, I have contributed this humble opinion, hoping that the members of the National Diplomacy Association will awaken the people of the Northeast and strive forward. I am not talented, but I am also very willing to follow the comrades and struggle together.

Wuxi 76

The Issue of Affixing Stamps to Business Licenses After the government reduced the likin, various provinces are implementing business tax, which is about to be levied. The stamp, tobacco, and alcohol tax bureaus of Zhejiang, Hunan, and other provinces have asked the Ministry of Finance how to handle the affixing of stamps to business licenses applied for by various businesses. The Ministry has decided that those with capital of more than 500 yuan should affix a stamp worth 5 jiao per license, and those with capital of less than 500 yuan should affix a stamp worth 1 jiao 5 fen per license. The provincial bureaus have issued orders to the various branch bureaus to comply with this. The Wuxi Stamp Tax Branch Bureau has also received the provincial order and forwarded it to the County Chamber of Commerce for assistance. The Chamber of Commerce has replied, stating that the Chambers of Commerce of various counties recently held a meeting in Zhenjiang to discuss the business tax issue, and this case was thoroughly discussed. It was unanimously believed that the principle of stamp tax is to prove rights, while the business license is a public certificate given to merchants who pay business tax, which is only sufficient to prove obligations, not rights, and is the same as the receipt issued to people who pay land tax. There is no need to affix stamps. Since the business tax is being levied for the first time, merchants still have objections to the tax rate, and many are hesitant to register for licenses. If they are forced to pay stamp tax again, it may not be beneficial to the stamp tax, and it will be an obstacle to the business tax. It was decided to jointly submit a report to the Ministry by the Chambers of Commerce of all provinces to request cancellation. Yesterday, the Stamp Tax Bureau was informed of the situation for its reference.

Electricity Price Increase The Qishuyan Power Plant is affected by the rising prices of gold and the devaluation of silver, as well as the soaring prices of various electrical materials. Fuel coal, which is the raw material for power generation, accounts for more than 50% of the total expenditure. This year's market price is more than one or two higher than in previous years, and the electricity price is still collected at a 10% discount from the set price, resulting in significant losses. It has been decided to collect the full price of 1 jiao 8 fen from May 1 to compensate for the losses. The county government and the Chamber of Commerce have been notified separately for their information.

Tongxinchang Paper Shop Sealed Up The Tongxinchang Paper Shop, located on Daqiao Street outside the North Gate, has been in operation for more than 60 years. The major shareholder is Peng Jingchu from Suzhou, and the manager is Peng Zhongpei. At the end of last year, due to poor turnover, it went bankrupt, owing a total of more than 100,000 yuan. The Shaoxing foil merchants and the local money shops in Wuxi have successively filed lawsuits with the County Court, and the money shop representative Cai Yourong and others twisted Peng Zhongpei to the Fifth Branch Bureau of Public Security, and transferred him to the County Public Security Bureau for transfer to the County Court for interrogation. Because there was no cash guarantee of 60,000 yuan, he was immediately detained for interrogation. Yesterday, the County Court sent Secretary Liu, together with various creditors, to Daqiao Street and Luhua Lane to seal up the shop and warehouse successively, pending liquidation and repayment.

Zhenjiang 78

Now, the Finance Department, considering the urgent deadline, has specifically scheduled a meeting on the 10th of this month to gather representatives from ten counties with the most abandoned farmland, including Zhenjiang, Jintan, Liyang, Nantong, Haimen, Changshu, Lishui, Jurong, Kunshan, and Wu County, to discuss the measures together to facilitate the process. Therefore, a copy of the list has been issued to the various counties for detailed investigation, and a separate list should be prepared and brought to the province to determine the standard.

Various Trade Tax Rules Associations Telegraph Request for Revision of Business Tax Rates 85

The Tax Rate Shall Not Exceed Two Per Thousand

The Whole Sale Part Shall Be Taxed at One Quarter

The Tax Rules Research Committee of the city's various trade associations telegraphed the Ministry of Finance on the 3rd regarding the business tax, saying, "To the Nanjing National Government Ministry of Finance, We have learned that the outline of the business tax and supplementary measures stipulates that for those who use the amount of business as the tax standard, the maximum shall not exceed two per thousand, and those who use the amount of capital as the tax standard, the maximum shall not exceed twenty per thousand. The meaning is very clear. However, after reading the business tax rates of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces revised by the Ministry, except for grain, oil, salt, firewood, charcoal, and planning industries, all exceed the maximum amount of two per thousand. The intention is to speculate that the outline has provisions on luxury businesses and those that contain the nature of being banned, so this exceeds the maximum tax rate. However, after examining the commodities that pay five or ten per thousand tax, such as the paint industry, water cement industry, industry, rubber industry, etc., most of them are necessary for daily use or belong to the scope that should be promoted. The tax rate should be reduced to conform to the central government's original intention of cutting likin. Moreover, at the beginning of this tax system reform, it is especially appropriate to avoid the heavy and take the light to make it easy to promote and benefit. However, it is heard that the tax rates proposed by the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau are also based on the first revision by the Ministry, which violates the provisions of the outline, increases the burden on merchants and citizens, and Shanghai has special circumstances, which cannot be compared with other provinces. The implementation of the business tax is only an accidental income. It is not the same as other provinces that have suffered losses from the cut likin. The implementation of the business tax is only an accidental income. It is not the same as other provinces that have suffered losses from the cut likin. The implementation of the business tax is only an accidental income. It is not the same as other provinces that have suffered losses from the cut likin. The implementation of the business tax is only an accidental income. It is not the same as other provinces that have suffered losses from the cut likin. Low taxes do not hinder the progress of municipal administration, and high taxes are enough to困營the survival of the industry. The right to gain and loss should be based on the economy. Moreover, Shanghai's business market is prosperous in other provinces. The competition in the same industry is also very fierce. Business operators mostly aim at small profits and cheap sales. The tax burden should be relatively light. The business tax contains the nature of income tax. According to the situation, it cannot be taxed too high. Moreover, the region has the separation of concessions, and the shops have purely foreign capital. In order to achieve a universal and average burden, the tax rate must be reduced so that merchants and citizens are happy to donate and contribute to the government's tax revenue. The former Secretary-General of the Municipal Government Yu Hongjun said that Mayor Zhang meant that if Shanghai holds a business tax in the future, the tax rate will not be higher than the regulations of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, or even slightly lower than it to reduce the burden on citizens. It is enough to see the crux of the problem. Although the city's merchants are in a state of business depression, if the tax rate is indeed in line with the provisions of the outline approved by the Executive Yuan, they should be able to understand the good intentions of the authorities to care for the people's livelihood and strive to pay taxes. If the provisions of the outline are used as a proviso and become an unlimited heavy tax, it cannot be an excessive burden, hinder the survival of one's own business, and绝the future tax revenue of the country. It is reasonable to submit a telegram to appeal, urging the Department to revise the business tax rates of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces again, and to correct the tax rate when the city's business tax rate is requested for approval. The tax rate shall not exceed two per thousand, and the wholesale part shall still maintain the original draft of the Shanghai Municipality and be taxed at one quarter to reduce the burden and benefit the commercial industry. At the end of the telegram, I cannot wait to receive orders, The Tax Rules Research Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Industry Association叩Jiang."

Exemption from Business Tax Items 86

Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai Silk Joint Association

Telegram Request for Supplementary Interpretation

The Joint Association of Silk Fabric Trade Associations of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai, yesterday sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, requesting supplementary interpretation of various issues regarding the exemption from business tax. The original telegram stated: "Respectfully to the Nanjing Ministry of Finance, regarding the business tax on silk fabrics, your Ministry, in accordance with the Central Government's intention, has uniformly reduced the proposed tax rate for Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Hubei provinces to two per thousand, demonstrating your utmost concern for protecting domestic products and caring for agriculture and commerce, which is deeply admired. However, regarding the exemption portion, supplementary interpretation from your Ministry is needed to avoid misunderstandings during collection in various provinces and cities. We respectfully submit the following details: (1) The exemption of business tax for wholesale businesses directly established by manufacturers has already been approved in your Ministry's document Fu Zi No. 5675, communicated by telegram to the Shanghai Silk Fabric Trade Association. However, according to item one of the five-point notification on key points of business tax interpretation issued by your Ministry, it is stipulated that provinces shall not levy business tax on factories or companies that have already paid consolidated tax or special consumption tax, but commercial firms and shops engaged in promotion and sales shall still be subject to business tax. The so-called commercial firms and shops engaged in promotion and sales specifically refer to those engaged in retail sales. The so-called wholesale businesses directly established by factories or companies, regardless of whether they use the name of a commercial firm or shop due to commercial practices, should all follow the telegram approval and be exempt from business tax. This is the first item requiring supplementary interpretation. (2) Wholesale businesses directly established by manufacturers have now been approved for exemption from business tax. Therefore, the scope of 'manufacturer' should be broadly defined. Large-scale silk factories and handicraft workshops are both manufacturers in nature. In terms of capability, workshops are even weaker than factories. If wholesale outlets directly established by silk factories can be exempt from business tax, then wholesale distribution centers jointly entrusted to agents by workshops, commonly known as silk stores, should also be exempt. This is the second item requiring supplementary interpretation. (3) The exemption of business tax for brokers who only buy and do not sell has also been approved in your Ministry's document Fu Zi No. 5754, communicated by telegram to the Shanghai Various Industries Tax Regulations Research Committee, stating that brokers who only buy and do not sell have no business income and are naturally not subject to collection, and are not listed in the business tax regulations submitted by Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, so there is no cause for dispute. However, we fear that without a clear regulation, collecting officials may have misunderstandings. This is the third item requiring supplementary interpretation. Regarding the above three items, we respectfully request your Ministry's approval and issuance of a general order to all provinces and cities to comply with, so as to avoid disputes through common understanding. We anxiously await your instructions. Sincerely, the Preparatory Office of the Joint Association of Silk Fabric Trade Associations of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai, bows."

Second Day of the Fisheries Improvement Promotion Conference 87

Yesterday (the 5th) was the second day of the Jiangsu Province and Shanghai City Fisheries Improvement Promotion Conference, still held at the Minli Middle School in Xiaonanmen. Due to recreational performances, the number of attendees was even greater than on the first day. The situation at the venue is recorded below:

Venue Situation: The venue opened at 9:00 AM for people to view various exhibits. Recreational performances began at 1:00 PM, with programs including a costumed speech by a youth propaganda team, fishermen's songs and dances, and fisheries films, including (1) "Exploring the Sea," (2) "Ocean Wonders," (3) "Warm-Water Fish Situation," and (4) "Whaling Situation," in four reels. Marine products, animals, plants, and various fishing boats and gear were rare items, so the viewers were extremely crowded. At 2:30 PM, the entrance was announced to be closed. Even at 4:00 PM, people continued to arrive in an endless stream, vying to rush in. Despite the polite persuasion of the conference staff, the noise was deafening, and the situation was turbulent. Some even climbed over the walls to enter. Fearing an accident, the conference stopped the recreational performances, and the situation calmed down. The performances continued again around 7:00 PM in the evening. In total, no less than 9,000 people attended yesterday morning. Furthermore, to attract the interest of the guests, the conference stipulated a prize-giving method: each ticket entitled one person to draw a lot once, with a modest gift of cuttlefish, small yellow croaker, prawns, etc., totaling 20,000 tickets. Among them, the numbers with prizes were 3,000. Yesterday, more than 1,000 numbers were drawn, it is said.

A Glimpse of the Exhibition: The exhibition area was divided into ten rooms. Rooms 1, 2, and 3 were for private products; Room 4 was for ocean meteorology and navigation items; Room 5 was for fishing gear and tackle; Room 6 was for old-style fisheries in coastal Jiangsu Province; Room 7 was for new-style fishing boats and nets from foreign countries; Room 8 was for water product division inscriptions; Room 9 was for new-style fisheries and fishing area models; and Room 10 was for water product manufactures, such as salt-cured, dried, and shellfish products, as well as water product economic charts. The visitors were led by water product expert Mr. Wang Defa, who toured each room and provided detailed explanations. Among the items on display, the models of Chinese coastal fishing grounds, the theodolite, the astronomical clock, and the national emblem made of shellfish were particularly rare. Overall, the arrangement of each room was rich in artistic flair.

Staff Meeting: Due to the large number of visitors, the conference was unable to provide adequate reception, and to expand publicity, it was decided that staff should be temporarily added. Therefore, an emergency meeting was held at 12:00 PM. The attending committee members were Cai Hengru, Hou Chaohai, Zhou Jianyin, Wang Wentai, Zhou Hanmei, etc. The following five proposals were agreed upon:

(1) Request the Public Security Bureau to send eight more police officers to maintain order at the recreational performance and prize-giving lottery. (2) Assign staff to the recreational performance venue and various exhibition rooms. (3) Hire additional water product experts to give lectures. (4) Print more publications to expand publicity. (5) Assign a special representative to receive news reporters.

Today's Program: In addition to continuing the exhibition and recreational performances, the conference will also invite representatives from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, as well as water product expert Mr. Li Dongpu, to give a lecture entitled "Strategies for Improving China's Fisheries," it is said.

The Consolidated Tax Administration of the Ministry of Finance, previously due to repeated requests from the cloth industry to issue transport permits for inspection and release, in order to be especially considerate of commercial transport difficulties, approved that all directly woven products with the original cotton yarn fixed tax certificate can also apply for transport permits for customs inspection and release. The industry has been able to conveniently declare exports since April 1. Unexpectedly, merchants in various inland cloth producing regions are dissatisfied. The reason is that since handmade native cloth is exempt from tax, this procedure could have been omitted, resulting in more than thirty documents from the Jiangyin, Wujin, and Wuxi county chambers of commerce, as well as the native cloth industry associations of various provinces, requesting the Ministry of Finance Consolidated Tax Administration to stop issuing transport permits. It is now heard that the local cloth industry believes that after this native cloth is exempt from tax, holding a transport document with a regional certification of origin will prevent difficulties along the way. Now, the Consolidated Tax Administration is instructing local industry associations to apply for the transport permits from the Consolidated Tax Administration Bureau, which is a more complete procedure. The opposition from the native cloth industries in various places is a misunderstanding. The course of events is specifically sent to various chambers of commerce to inform all colleagues in the native cloth industry, to avoid disputes, it is said.

Consolidated Tax Administration Stipulates Drawback Method for Dispatch Notes 94

The Consolidated Tax Administration of the Ministry of Finance sent a letter to the Chinese Yarn Factory Association, stating: "Respectfully to the recipient, it is hereby ordered by the Ministry of Finance that, prior to the establishment of the consolidated tax on cotton yarn (February 1), if merchants have prepaid customs duties and the customs dispatch notes they hold have not been used up by April 15 of this year, and if the customs duties that should have been stopped are paid with said dispatch notes after the consolidated tax was collected, but before the customs implemented the method of exempting customs duties for items on which the consolidated tax has already been collected, the Consolidated Tax Administration will refund the amount. However, if merchants have obtained dispatch notes from customs after the consolidated tax was established on February 1, and the dispatch notes are still in the merchants' hands, or have already been used to pay customs duties that should have been stopped, the customs will refund the amount uniformly. It should be obeyed. However, the amount of consolidated tax that each yarn factory should pay monthly is usually cleared at the end of the month. If there are any of the above circumstances, please submit a special case to the Consolidated Tax Administration for the drawback dispatch notes, and after verification, a reply will be given and the amount will be issued in accordance with the regulations. It is not necessary to deduct the amount yourself when settling the tax payment, in order to clarify the amount and avoid confusion. In addition to sending a separate document, a corresponding document is hereby sent for your review and to inform all manufacturers."

The Shanghai Sausage Industry Association sent a telegram yesterday to the National Government Ministry of Finance and Ministry of Industry and Commerce, stating: "Respectfully to the National Government Ministry of Finance and Ministry of Industry and Commerce, pig, cattle, and sheep intestines in our country are one of our native products. After being manufactured into finished products by hand, they are transported to countries such as Germany, France, and the United States for sales, relying on this trade to make a living. There are tens of thousands of people across the country. Since the sixteenth year of the Republic, the number of these trades has decreased year by year, and industry and commerce have also been in a state of difficulty. The export trade of so-called cattle and sheep intestines has been in a slump, and the amount of trade is actually close to nothing. However, the pig intestine business is also in a precarious state. The reason is that the export tariff is too high, which is a major blow. Moreover, in the past two years, the customs tax assessment has often exceeded the actual selling price, resulting in another layer of hidden losses. If this continues without seeking relief, it will inevitably be completely eliminated. Thinking of this, we cannot help but shudder. After repeated deliberation, we can only respectfully request that when your ministry formulates export tariffs, the export tax on pig intestines be specially reduced and listed as an example of three per cent of the value. We have always admired your ministry's concern for people's livelihood and consideration for industry and commerce, so we are taking the liberty of sending a telegram to appeal. We implore you to examine and approve our request. We anxiously await your instructions. Sincerely, the Shanghai Sausage Industry Association."
