French Tennis Open 159

Tennis King Henri Cochet Did Not Participate

Japanese Players Win Both Singles and Doubles Titles

(Paris Dispatch) This year's Davis Cup competition is about to begin, and players from various countries are now conserving their energy and preparing to compete with each other. France is particularly enthusiastic about tennis. The Poissy Cup Tennis Tournament was held in Canus on March 26, with players from England, Germany, France, Japan, and other countries participating. However, French tennis king Henri Cochet personally declined to participate in the tournament, intending to give the opportunity to those who came from afar. The Japanese players who attended were Sato Hyotaro and Sato Tsuyoshi. The two hurriedly participated in the tournament immediately after arriving in France. Sato Tsuyoshi was eliminated by the British player Rhodes by a score of 3-0 in the second week of the competition, while Sato Hyotaro fought bravely alone and passed several rounds in a row. On the 29th of this month, Rhodes and Sato Hyotaro met in the final. Rhodes was a British Davis Cup player, while Sato was the captain of the Japanese Davis Cup team. The two were very skilled. After four sets of fierce fighting, Sato Hyotaro won by a score of 3-1 and won the singles title. During the match, Rhodes took the lead and won the first set. After that, Sato won three sets in a row with a determined effort. The last set was a decisive moment for both sides, and the performance was particularly amazing. The French tennis king visited the stadium that day and said that Japan would not be difficult to become the future leader of world tennis. The singles results are recorded below:

Sato Hyotaro (Japan) 3-6, 6-4, 6-1, 8-6 Rhodes (England)

In the doubles, the teams that won the final were the French and Japanese teams. The French team was Nishimura and Hejier, and the Japanese team was the two Satos. During the final, the Japanese players won easily, with a result of 3-0. The results are as follows:

Sato Hyotaro, Sato Tsuyoshi (Japan) 6-1, 6-4, 6-4 Nishimura, Hejier (France) This competition was the first time that Japan attended this year's Davis Cup, and it was a rare achievement to win both the singles and doubles titles in France, which shocked Europe and the United States. I recall that in 1928, our country's Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai returned home to participate in the Eighth Far Eastern Games and won both the singles and doubles titles. At that time, our country's strength was comparable to that of Japan. In the past three years, Japan has vigorously promoted tennis, and outstanding players have emerged frequently. They also attend the Davis Cup every year and have now become a strong enemy of Europe and the United States. On the contrary, in our country, players are sitting back and falling behind due to economic reasons. Is this not a pity?

Expenses for the North China Games 166

Shandong Provincial Government Approves Over 91,000 Yuan

—Sports Field to Be Completed by the 20th—

Jinan Correspondence: The athletic field for the 15th North China Games, held at the Shandong Provincial Public Sports Ground, is undergoing full-scale renovations that began some time ago. With the games drawing near, and the Shandong Games being held here in advance for preliminary selections, the timeframe is even tighter. The Public Works Bureau and contractors are actively discussing methods to ensure completion within the pre-determined schedule. This morning (3rd), Director of Education He Siyuan and Director of Construction Zhang Honglie visited the site, accompanied by Zhang Yixian, Director of the Public Sports Ground, to inspect the entire field. They urged the completion of all venues as quickly as possible, without delay. The current schedule stipulates that earthwork must be completed by April 10th, athletic field construction by April 20th, and full field layout by April 30th. If the time is too short for complete completion, the western viewing stand for important guests should be repaired first to avoid disrupting its use. It is hoped that the entire project can be completed on schedule as planned. Furthermore, as the North China Preparatory Committee's date approaches, the organization and order divisions' director, Mr. Shang Shumei, attended. The North China football and basketball events will remain in Beiping. A letter was sent yesterday urging them to come to Shandong to guide everything. Mr. Yuan Xiaoli, a North China sports expert, is also reportedly coming to Jinan. The games' expenses are 16,921 yuan, and the sports field construction budget is 74,275.435 yuan. These were reviewed and reported by the Finance, Construction, and Education Bureaus a few days ago. Today (3rd), the provincial government's regular meeting passed the original proposal. The games' expenses will be drawn from the 19th year's budget's temporary line item for the North China Games and provincial school games and education reserve fund. The construction expenses will be drawn from the provincial reserve fund.

The Shandong Education Bureau has organized a North China preliminary selection preparatory committee to participate in the 15th North China Games. The 10th North China Games preliminary selection will be held from May 6th. The Education Bureau states that this province has held provincial secondary school games in previous years. This year's preliminary selection is for participation in the North China Games. In addition to provincial, county, and municipal officially recognized private secondary schools, amateur groups may also participate. However, the name "North China Preliminary Selection" seems too narrow, so it has been changed to the Shandong Provincial Games. Last year's spring games are considered the first, and this session is the second. Notices have already been sent to various schools. However, the games regulations will still apply to the promulgated preliminary selection regulations.

Last Week's Gold Market Showed Rapid Advances 169

The progress was very smooth. Last week, the gold market saw a significant rise, almost reaching its peak. The pace was brisk, moving forward all the way. At the beginning of the week, due to large accounts such as Xinheng Yuansheng selling off and the easing of exchange rates, the lowest price suddenly fell to 686 taels. The inner market of banks also tended to improve, with colleagues making up positions and shorting bars. Currently, major speculative accounts such as Yuancheng Xinheng (Luo) had previously held short positions and have now covered. Hengxing Yuan (Lu) and Wu are in long positions. The Guangdong syndicate seems flat. According to the daily gold settlement price, the result was around 60 taels, ranging from 70 to 40 taels. Spot goods were about 9 taels higher. The Art World

Surrealist Painting 173

— Hai Yan

Surrealism (Sur Realisme) is the name of a new poetry movement that originated in the French poetry scene recently. This movement also affected painters with similar tendencies. Therefore, the Surrealist movement in the French art scene has also risen.

According to their claims, Surrealism is based on the belief in certain forms that have been forgotten, the excellent reality of association, the omnipotence of dreams, and all indifferent intellectual activity.

Surrealism is a worldview that recognizes the world and provides fundamental ideas. Its theory is based on the discourse of Henri Bergson and is based on Freud's psychoanalysis.

Natural science, of course, denies the world outside the phenomena within the scope of time and space. However, this is limited to the realm of reality. In addition, in our spiritual life, there is still the creative function beyond the laws of nature. Based on material experience based on observation and experience, we arrive at the truth of things according to spiritual life or intuition - Bergson's philosophy is where the Surrealists express their sympathy.

Freud's exploration of the unconscious world, especially the interpretation of dreams, also gave them great stimulation. They want to extract the essence of the spirit from the dreams of unconscious spiritual function, induce the state of dreams that transcends reality and the realm of consciousness into the real world, and create a new world. That is painting, that is poetry. They do not regard this kind of association as the subordination of dreams to reality as it has always been, but treat it as an absolute phenomenon of dreams themselves.

Surrealists not only want to abandon the aesthetics since the Italian Renaissance, but also hold the vitality to exclude the Latin foundation of reality. They despise the laws of harmony, ignore the dogmas of classical constraints, and stand on the front line of France's avant-garde soldiers - Surrealists - seeing the spirit as if it were everyday speech. As a result, the qualifications for the existence of romantic discussions, which have been despised by the radical painters of today, and regarded as astonishingly mysterious and inner life, are re-cultivated. They love the irrational, intuitive, and simple forms of expression of art.

A passage from the Surrealist manifesto says, "Surrealism is not satisfied with the expression of a certain school or a certain hometown. It integrates the reasons for the division of Europe and the elements of its existence. It must absorb all the doctrines in the world. Surrealism is a major movement in modern times. It means health and easily overcomes the tendency of decline and weakness."

The representative painters of Surrealism are Giorgio de Chirico, Max Ernst, Joan Miro, Andre Massno, etc.

Chirico is regarded as the leader of the team. He was born in Volos, Greece in 1888. Although he is an Italian, he has Sicilian blood flowing through him. He is a self-taught painter. He used to live in Munich and returned to Rome due to the war. Later, he moved to Paris where he currently lives.

He despised many young talented painters who gathered under the Futurists and Impressionists. Whether it was Impressionism, Fauvism, or Absolutists, he did not participate in any of them, nor did he fall into literary chants. He understood the intellectual spiritual principles of great classical art with his profound knowledge, and explored the pure tradition of past paintings. As a mystic and poet, he observed the universe with his own eyes and experienced the universe with his unique heart. He created new compositions from the traditional classical past of his motherland. Indeed, Chirico's works cleverly utilize the inherent donation of classical traditions and succeed in becoming astonishing crystallizations of fantasy. He combines light, color, and shadow to construct contrasting lines and spaces. The creation of that sculptural form gives a unique new value to ancient and modern habits.

Chirico observes dreams as if they were mathematics, and transforms dreams into reality with magical geometry. His recent dreams have repeatedly appeared like galloping horses.

He was once called a metaphysical school because of metaphysical realism. Today, he is a Surrealist, but his inherent nature does not change because of this.

Ernst, born in 1891 in Brühl in the Rhine region of Germany, studied at Dusseldorf and now lives in Paris. He is interested in all plastic arts. Sometimes he paints, sometimes he engages in sculpture, and sometimes he strives to compose photographic experiments.

In his work in 1922, there is a painting called "Group Portrait". Although it cannot be given extra praise, it is interesting to depict a group of Surrealist poets in Paris. In addition to more than a dozen poets in different forms, sculptured Chirico and Raphael are also depicted in this group.

He is not only endowed with the talent of a painter, but also has the excellent talent of a printmaker. In 1922, he published two print collections in Paris, "Clichés" and "Eternal Misfortune", with a preface by Eluard Paul. Recently, a collection of paintings entitled "Natural History" has been published. This collection of paintings has a preface by Dada poet Arp. It collects thirty-four true descriptions of the creative history of fantasy nature. This work is extremely impressive. There is a "Human Eye" inside, microscopically enlarging and depicting the human eye. It should be said that he discovered an artistic field that predecessors had never set foot in. His keen sense has succeeded in opening up such a new realm.

Generally speaking, it is more appropriate to say that his other works are bizarre rather than clever and surprising. However, there, it makes us marvel at how vast his dream world is.

Miro, a Spaniard, is a bright lyric painter. His passion is as hot as a raging fire, and his love is as sweet as honey. Therefore, Miro's imagination is like the mystery of the moonlit night, but its expression is as clear as daylight. Miro's lyrical talent and Surrealist spirit are fused together, which is enough to play an amazing piece of SurRealisme music. He likes to describe the working world in front of him, and his works include "Hotel", "Family", "Circus", etc.

Masson's personality is like a new sprout of a branch, tempted by the spring breeze and fluttering. Although his works do not have the truth of Ernst, they are always soft and dreamlike. His style often has a French feel, very similar to George Braque, such as "Indoor Nude", "Knife", "Fish Struggle" and other works, all with a soft viscosity.

In addition to Giorgio de Chirico, Max Ernst, Joan Miro, Andre Masson, and others, the representative writers of Surrealism also include Dablskog, Yyos Tanguy, Francis Picabia, and German Walter Spios, Mensean, and American M Ray, etc.

During the consideration period, with the vague tendency of Surrealist sympathy, Pablo Plcasso, Goorges Braque, and Paul Klee are regarded as honorary members of Surrealism. The first two are the pioneers of Cubism, and the latter is the fierce general who remains in Expressionism. The three have firmly established their reputation in the modern art world, but it is inevitable that the changes in the background of the times will shake their inherent foundations.

This weak introduction is dedicated to friends who are enthusiastic about emerging art.

Tisei Pattern Exhibition 174

— Gang

In China, where the atmosphere of art - especially patterns - is very thin, a pattern exhibition of the Tisei Society has recently been held in Shanghai. This is such a delightful thing.

The Tisei Pattern Society is organized by the students of the Pattern Department of the West Lake Art College. They not only put in hard work on skills, but also try to explore new ways of patterns in this wilderness of China, and make a lot of research on pattern theory.

Oriental (Chinese) patterns have had a glorious history in the world art scene, but now they have declined. In modern times, Western mechanical civilization has also rushed to the East like a spring tide. Therefore, domestic goods are rejected because of their crudeness and clumsiness. Although this reason is due to the backwardness of the Chinese economy, the lack of beautiful patterns to organize complete goods and compete with foreign goods is also a fact. So, if we want to improve the international economic status and beautify the lives of the masses, we must incidentally promote patterns to develop mechanical industries. It must be that the gentlemen of the Tisei Society are willing to organize the pattern society and hold exhibitions with painstaking efforts, and they must have resolutely added this important mission to their own shoulders, and hope to attract the attention of the masses in the country to patterns.

Again, as mentioned above, patterns are an art that develops more and more with material civilization, so it becomes more and more a utilitarian and practical thing with the evolution of cities. The items in this Tisei exhibition are all designs for practical objects, and in the expression of lines and colors in their works, it can be seen that they are well-trained, and they have found a new direction for Chinese patterns in many ways.

Naturally, in China, where all art is backward, remote patterns are even more difficult to be recognized. However, this kind of applied art is always developing with the evolution of society, so I hope that the domestic pattern artists, especially the gentlemen of the Tisei Pattern Society, will continue to work hard to complete this cause.

Finally, I sincerely recommend that the public visit this pattern exhibition, because it is indeed a valuable gain in the barren pattern world of China.

Note: The Tisei Pattern Exhibition will be held at the National Goods Market on Nanjing Road for four days from the 3rd to the 6th of this month.

Art World Manuscript Guidelines 175

(1) Text should be limited to news, reviews, and introductions concerning recent art (painting, music, sculpture, architecture, drama, etc.) and literature from home and abroad.

(2) Photographs should be limited to recent portraits and works of artists from home and abroad, as well as various photographs related to words/text.

(3) The word count for each piece of text should not exceed 2,000 words.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) Write horizontally. Avoid writing in a sloppy manner. Western text should be omitted where possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(6) When including illustrations in the manuscript, do not use blue ink, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(7) Please indicate "Art World Editorial Department" on the submitted manuscript.

(8) Submitted manuscripts will not be returned, whether published or not. If return is required, it should be stated in advance with sufficient postage attached.

(9) Remuneration for text is divided into three categories: four yuan, three yuan, and two yuan per thousand words. The same applies to drawings and photographs per piece. Special manuscripts will be remunerated separately.

Youth Forum

The Poet's Moving 176

— Mo Zhi

Moving house is originally a very ordinary thing, and there is no need to record it. However, a poet's moving is very different from the so-called moving of ordinary people, as if it contains a kind of fun worth savoring. It is beautified, artistic, and can even be said to be full of poetic flavor. What I want to describe here is not my own moving, but me, a person who is not good at doing things, helping the poet × who is shaking the literary world to move house. Because I have always been an "outsider" to these things, I have been living alone in a small corner of a red building in Jiangwan for more than three years. My friends who lived with me have moved to other places from this red building one after another. Only I, the red building, have a reluctant feeling. On the other hand, moving also requires economics. Because I owe the landlord too much rent, because of this kind of restriction that outsiders cannot know, I have deeply thrown the matter of "moving" behind me. In fact, it can also be said that I am lazy by nature. A so-called lazy person is naturally not very fond of moving, so I think moving is a job that diligent people like to do.

A friend once jokingly asked me, "Mo, how long are you going to live in this old nest? I see you have never moved once, which is quite interesting."

I always answer them in my usual way, "Probably until I graduate from here, but I think the past four years are very easy to pass."

My friends are still skeptical, saying, "Not necessarily. You will graduate next summer, won't you have to move? I think you might continue to live here..."

"That won't happen," I interrupted, "So-called university graduation, although useless, but the maintenance of life is always very important. I am a poor young man. Not only do I have to find a relatively stable place to eat, but also take care of my family. The burden of my life is so heavy, of course I can't sit in this old nest and not seek new development. Really talking about moving house will cause sadness for the bleak future, so my cowardly heart hopes to never move..."

I often talk about these things with my friends. This time, the poet Yi, whom I respect, actually came to me for moving. Although I am not good at this, but because of the relationship of friendship, it is also my duty to do so. So, I happily agreed to him.

The poet's love for artistry is an extremely obvious fact. The poet Yi, whom I respect, of course cannot escape this example. On the noon of the day he moved, I ran to his place happily alone - a small building in Tiantong'an. I saw him sitting there smiling as usual, and he was humming Su Li Su Lu in his mouth as usual, probably reciting poetry. When he saw me coming, he stood up full of joy and shook hands with me. I also broke into a smile on my sad face.

"Why are things still so scattered? Are you moving today?" I asked suspiciously.

"The move is so-so," he said, followed by a burst of his usual poetic laughter.

"Great poet...artistic..." I praised him like this.

"Hee...hee...hee..." He then evoked the poet's smile.

I am as thin as firewood, and I really don't have the strength to do heavier things. This time, I only have to make an exception, and the two of us lay the bedding and tidy up the scattered items. As a result, it is still not very neat, and we are in a hurry and don't know what to do. But looking at these items that we consider to be tidied up, we finally feel that they are full of mysterious poetry. He himself only thought that besides deeply hiding the poetry manuscripts, which are more precious than his life, in his leather suitcase, almost all the other items are not so-called precious items in his eyes.

Really, only the poems that the poet hums are precious.

So, we ate the so-called "Yangchun noodles" that ordinary people eat in Shanghai in a very economical way. Because we did some work, we forgot that we were hungry. But after we finished eating this bowl of noodles, we still couldn't understand whether this life was "proletarian" or "poetic."

The moving truck came and carried us and all the poet's belongings to a certain road in the French Concession, which is where his new residence is located. His co-residents, such as Mr. Li and Mr. Zhang, are all famous people in the literary world today, and the place here is very quiet. If you create literary works, especially poetry, it is really the most suitable. I sincerely said, "Poet Yi, you should contribute more great poems to the Chinese literary world in the future!" He just smiled, and a poetic smile appeared on his round face.

After casually making his bed, we bid farewell to Mr. Li's virtuous wife and Mr. Zhang, who was busy editing the evening newspaper that had to be published that day, and wandered on the quiet road. I then realized that moving is originally such a thing.

At this time, it was already more than three o'clock, and we all felt a little hungry. He said that I was too tired today for his moving, and invited me to a small restaurant on North Sichuan Road, where several of us wandering loners often come to have a snack, so that we can talk about many things we want to say. In order to avoid rejecting the poet's kindness, I had to sincerely and happily bother him again.

We were very disappointed that we had not met Mr. Bao, who is respected by young people, otherwise our conversation would be more vigorous. However, on this day, the two of us talked until more than seven o'clock before leaving this memorable teahouse. After drinking, we were again intoxicated in the mysterious night on North Sichuan Road.

At this time, in addition to peeping at the displays in various stores, we never have the courage to appreciate the women on the road. Although poets are sometimes intoxicated in the net of love, we are all loners. Talking about love will cause infinite sadness, especially for people like me who wander the sea and have no relatives. Looking at my haggard face, I don't look like someone who hopes to pursue love. I should still work hard on my current career to seek the development of the country and nation, as well as my entire self. Thinking of this, the idea of love that young people urgently need is also dispelled invisibly. A certain poet is certainly much happier than me. His exquisite and lovely fiancée is studying in Suzhou, and the letters back and forth are express delivery, which is very worthy of being proud in front of me, a lonely wanderer.

After wandering for a long time, I felt a little lost, so I shook hands with the poet and said goodbye and returned to Jiangwan. It was already more than nine o'clock, but because my mind was confused, there are still a lot of so-called poetic things that have not been described to the fullest. Sometimes, the poet's nature is really too perverted, and it also makes us unable to tell why. I only feel that "poets are great."

Jiaotong University Organizes International Friendship Association 177

In view of the current backwardness of science and technology and the sluggishness of industry in our country, Jiaotong University believes that it is not enough to make up for our shortcomings without adopting the strengths of others. Therefore, the relationship between our country and various advanced countries must be very harmonious, so as to peep into their secrets. The school has the mission of building a new China. Engineering and construction talents should especially learn from Europe and the United States. Therefore, the school must hold meetings to welcome and host banquets to establish friendship when European and American commercial and industrial inspection groups come to Shanghai. Recently, the school has also decided to organize an International Friendship Association through the school affairs meeting. Its tasks include (1) liaison matters concerning Chinese and foreign industry, commerce, and education, (2) visits and introductions concerning Chinese and foreign industry and commerce, (3) communication of Chinese and foreign industrial and commercial academic studies, (4) exchange of professors and publications, (5) hosting foreign scholars and industrial and commercial experts. The organization plans to handle it jointly with domestic groups, and the president of the school will hire professors from the school or leaders of domestic groups as members. The number of members is tentatively set at twenty-one, and they have not yet been hired. After the association is established, its first task is to exchange professors with Oxford and Cambridge Universities in the United Kingdom in the near future (this matter was mentioned by the president of the school, Li Zhaohuan, when he hosted a banquet for the British Economic Inspection Group at the Dahua Hotel. The inspection group immediately agreed to return home and discuss it with the government. This matter can probably be done soon). The committee also plans to send one member to be stationed in London for a long time to manage all foreign liaison matters, because London is centrally located and has extremely convenient transportation to various advanced countries in Europe and the United States. This member will be rotated among the members once a year, and at the same time, the member can also intern and study abroad. After returning to China, they will gain new knowledge, which can benefit a lot when teaching professors and students. It is really a win-win situation. (Quan)
